mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have shortened them based on my intention and formed tools in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the case of swelling coming to the groin before, it is without pain or health;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en .ij. costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also that which comes straight to the two ribs, and one cannot cure anything else but what is directly related to the back, as I say;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en .i. leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And that the patient's illness extends up to his belly in one equal length, and there is no strain on him, so he does not blister;
puis fiche .i. tison au chief en terre forment, et .i. autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et .i. autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then place one coal in the fire pit and another at the feet on the ground form, and tie a band around his limbs near the illness, and another at the hips, and at the knees, and at the ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les .ij. tisons;	And two craftsmen know how to tie them, one at the head and the others at joints, among these two rods;
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	And be well closed, the rod as we have said, and the mirror put her palms on the spine form, until she regains consciousness.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de .iij. bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if she does not recover from this cure, take a board of three arms long, and place it over the body, and if the patient is on their side, support the head of the board over the spine, then place the middle of the table on the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu; et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And place the mirror's feet at the other end of the board, press well, until they regain consciousness on their side; and if you can see, do it at the wrist that turns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches .ij. tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez .ij. autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And you should place two spikes into the head of the afflicted limb from shoulder to elbow, and towards the joints two others, with each spike having about the width of a hand's length between them.
et ait en chescun tison .i. pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent; et entre chescuns .ij. tisons ait .i. tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en .ij. tornans .ij. petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And in each spike place one piece or fragment, where the bend is corrected, and have the spikes firmly in the ground so they do not move; and between each pair of two spikes have a single turning spike, with which to guide the correction, and place two short spikes of hand's length between the two bends to correct the bend.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	And then tie the bandage that is among the elbows at the bend towards the head, and the other strap towards the joints at the other bend, and each of the assistants corrects their bend along the entire bandage, and the masters place the spine evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de .iij. dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are even, place a desiccative plaster with plenty of egg white on it, and then add the ointment, and after that apply the paste from a tablet of one and three-quarters inches long. This helps to heal the swollen area and the healthy part of the spine, then bind it with a string as we have mentioned, and make use of subtle irritation until it is healed;
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant; et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc,	And if no improvement comes at the end of healing, you should administer softening and soothing medicines, with the paste that we have mentioned previously; and every time it is administered, use a piece of pork fat.
et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations; et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption: par aventure feroit venir la mort.	And if an appearance comes about at the base of the spine in the back, and you should take care that it is a dislocation; for it's the bone that protrudes outwards, so there shouldn't be any assumption made about it: by chance it could bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	On the dislocations of the hip
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures; et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc .iiij. parties: dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier; et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	Know that the joints of the hip and shoulder only produce dislocations, not fractures like other joints; and the joint of the hip is dislocated according to four parts: inside and outside, front and back; and more so from within, less in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation from within is that when one joins the diseased leg with the healthy one, it becomes longer, and the diseased knee opens further than the healthy one, and the diseased knee cannot bend to touch the fire.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it is when the leg is swollen due to an abscess, because the shoulder of the thigh arrives there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him who comes to death is that this event is contrary to what precedes.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement; toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	And the signs of him who goes before, are that his leg is well according to its completion; nonetheless, he does not double the knee without pain, and if you try to make him walk, he cannot move forward and holds back his urine, and swells up his ankle, and when he walks, he walks on his heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who goes behind, are that he cannot spread his knee, nor double it, and this leg is more twisted than the other one, and his ankle is softened, and the shoulder joint comes out under the ribs at the top of the back.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure; et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	The return of this sign of dislocation is that you should confirm that the dislocation is old and remains in its position, if there is no treatment; and it is not appropriate to have any assumption about it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des .iiij. manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre; par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	And for those where the dislocation is recent, and there are four ways of dislocation, if you hurry to return the joint and stretch it inwards and outwards, and move it right and left; by chance should it return, and no further treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles .i. ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a .ij. mains, ou a .i. liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then it is necessary that you apply one strong force, and hold the leg strongly with two hands, or on a strap that is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe; et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And with another application of force extend your hand over in such a way that it presses her hands under her armpits, then thrusts inward against the thigh; and one holds the head to the strap;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And stretch up and down all at once, until the patient is lifted off the ground at once, and stays hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This stretching method applies to four similar situations; and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is correct.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance. Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	If not, treatment should be given based on its resemblance. If the dislocation is in the pardedens (sternum), you must have the patient lie on his side with a healthy limb, then put the bandage on the root of the leg, and above the heart, then lift it upwards towards the heart and towards the strength;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment: si revenra a son leu maintenant; et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	Then take another minister and hold both his arms, encircle the large part of the diseased leg with your arms, and extend it upwards in this form: if it returns to its position now; and this type of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les .ij. piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les .ij. talons, et sus les .ij. genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue .ij. dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot compress it in this way as we said, then you should tie the two legs of the affected side together with a tight string above both ankles and knees, so that the affected leg is extended by more than one span compared to the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre .ij. bras de lonc; puis comande a .j. ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then have it hung from the head of a post, and let there be two spans above the ground; then command one assistant to embrace the head of the leg, while another assistants hold on with the affected part, embracing to form the leg, for the joint is now coming back quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne .i. liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is at the front, if the leg lies down as we said in that with agility, and forces one string properly onto the affected leg and also on the foot;
puis met .ij. tisons, .i. au chief et .i. autre as piez, puis fiche .i. tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two twigs, one on the head and another at the elbow, then stick a twig between the armpits of the patient in the shape;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have planted wet cloths around him, to not blister the patient's skin, then extend each doctor towards him, and place them evenly by his hand for the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin. Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it comes back, it's good. If not, place him on a table, and press him like we said in the stomach treatment, and lay the patient on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is in front, it should be extended immediately as far as possible, and according to what I said; and place the patient's pain on the wrong side, then press with the other hand, and extend down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les .ij. hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the back, it does not need to extend the limb downwards or lift him from the ground, but he should be positioned just as when his hip was reset at the back, which is similar to us saying about lying on both hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and so on his face, and the limb should be extended as we have said previously, and must be pressed against the joint to the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	and it will be right when the patient extends his legs and they are equal; then adjust the thighs, place the plaster, and tie with a bandage, so that the hip does not move.
et se repose .iij. jors ou .iiij., puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse. iij. jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and let him rest for three or four days, then release the bandage and place the plaster; and if you see that they are equal, tighten again as before, and leave him for three more days; then release the bandage, and make him walk properly, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the hip
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The hip joint can be dislocated in three ways: one might say inside and outside, and behind; and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs for this are to instruct the patient to bend their leg at their knee, and if they cannot reach their knee, you know that their hip is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all this is to make the patient sit straight, and extend their leg if they can, and place your back on their buttocks, and put their foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les .ij. costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	Then take your knee bone in your hands and remove it between your fingers, then bend them two ribs formed by the knee. And another attendant extends his foot until the knees return to their place, and signs show that he has moved his leg lightly towards his thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort .iij. jors ou iiij., puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and place the plaster, and let the leg heat near the thigh, and join them tightly together for three or four days, then release; and do not disturb the injured parts while they heal, until the limbs are strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the limbs are not yet ready, apply strong extension, as we have said in treating the hip joint, until they recover.
de la dislocation dou talon	From the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes partially dislocated and sometimes fully out, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs for this are that the ankle swells, and bends forward towards the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The restoration of movement is easy, and you should gently extend it with your hands when it is only partially dislocated.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne .i. ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, then you should have the patient lie straight, and hold them one and a half ministers forward by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre .ij. fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then pull their foot towards you with your right hand, and then also with the left twice, then stretch them upwards, and firmly press the foot up high.
et fai ce .ij. fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	and do this twice, just as we have said, by pressing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is well; if not, restart the process, for it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche .i. passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return like that, then have the patient stand behind their back on the ground, and place two sticks firmly in the ground between their buttocks, and tie them with a cloth so they don't hurt the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a .i. liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the surgeons scorch the leg, and some other surgeons extend his foot to his hands or between two sticks,
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then extend each surgeon equally, and the pincers should be placed between the legs of the patient for holding the patient when they are extended.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then place the mirrors equally at the dislocation on his hands, and some other surgeons will scorch the healthy leg near the wound, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it has reached the point, place the plaster and bind it on top, then firmly secure it in position, and tie the knot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are behind the ankle, so they do not become too tight.
puis le laisse .ij. jors ou .iij., et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par .iiij. jors;	and leave it for two or three days, and if the knot unties, then tighten it again; then release it on the third day or fourth, and advise the patient to walk for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he walks beyond that limit, it's not secure that he won't dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when abscesses begin to drain, you should soothe them as we have said in other parts of the text, while they are still clean.
des dois	Of the cautery tool directed by fire, command the patient to let their hairs grow long and uniform; and if they start pricking at their base, keep the eyes steady so they don't move until they fully grow.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, if they should be nicely extended for work, it is a simple task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus .i. leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocations are in neither the back nor the feet, it should be that you have the patient sit on their full length or on their table completely straight, and place your foot where the joints spread open, then press with your foot firmly until they revive.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a .ij. chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse .iij. jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when they are equal, and there is no opening, one places under the foot of the patient a board for two shoulders, then holds them in place, and leaves it for three days, then releases it; and makes him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound accompanies the dislocation, and it needs to be restored, many times the patient has died:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not modest in the treatment, and if you are not skilled in the art or have not used it for a long time, and if you are not merciful and patient, do not be rash;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And when beginning with soothing things for an abscess, allow the patient to hold their hand on God's mercy, if you do not see hope for recovery.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, then immediately reset the limb in its place, so that the abscesses are relieved and healed.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is in its place, administer soothing remedies for abscesses, and treat the wound, as it should be treated, using desiccated ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is also dislocation and breaking of small bones, set the bones, and do what we have said about simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors. Amen	And protect yourself from the path of fear, according to what I have said, for this is your duty as per your Creator, and through knowledge you arm and fortify your body. Amen
Explicit le romen de fisique	End the chapter on anatomy
